	<script>

		jQuery.fn.center = function () {
			this.css("position","absolute");
			this.css("top", Math.max(0, (($(window).height() - this.outerHeight()) / 2) + $(window).scrollTop()) + "px");
			this.css("left", Math.max(0, (($(window).width() - this.outerWidth()) / 2) + $(window).scrollLeft()) + "px");
			return this;
		}


		window.alert = function(msg) {

			$('#notification-shim, #notification').remove();
			$('body').append('&lt;div id="notification-shim" style=""&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
			$('body').append([
				'&lt;div class="pane" id="notification"&gt;',
					'&lt;div id="notification-content"&gt;',
						msg,
						'&lt;div id="notification-buttonbar"&gt;',
							'&lt;button class="blue" onclick="$(\'#notification-shim\').click();"&gt;Close&lt;/button&gt;',
						'&lt;/div&gt;',
					'&lt;/div&gt;',
				'&lt;/div&gt;'
			].join(''));

			$('#notification').center();
			$('#notification-shim').show();
			$('#notification').fadeIn(500);

			$('#notification-shim').click(function(){

				$('#notification-shim, #notification').remove();

			});

		}

	</script>

                tid: channelId
            });
            ads.init();
        };

        this.init = function() {
            if (!scriptCalled) {
                scriptCalled = true;
                $.getScript('http://ox-d.zam.com/w/1.0/jstag');
            }
            if (typeof OX == 'undefined') {

                inst = ad_i[ad.auid] = OX(ad);
                inst.addHook(ads.onLoad, OX.Hooks.ON_ADUNIT_INITIALIZED);
                inst.load();
            }
        };

    <script>

    var skinSplitLoaded = false;
	function addSkinSplit() {
		$('body').css('background-color', '#000');
		$detach1 = $('#container').children().first().detach();
		$('#container').css('margin-top', '182px').prepend('&lt;div style="height: 10px;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
		$detach2 = $('#container #container_inner').children().slice(0, 2).detach();
		$('#container').parent().prepend($('&lt;div id="container" class="container-1"&gt;&lt;div id="container_inner" class="container_inner-1"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="height: 5px;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;'));
		$('.container-1').prepend($detach1);
		$('.container_inner-1').append($detach2);
	}

    function postSkinSetup(campaignId) {
        if (campaignId &amp;&amp; !skinSplitLoaded) {
            skinSplitLoaded = true;
			if( $.isReady ) {
				addSkinSplit();
			} else {
				$(function(){
					addSkinSplit();
				});
			}
        }
    }

					<script>

					$(function(){

						//https://github.com/odhyan/trie/blob/master/trie.js
						Trie=function(){this.words=0;this.prefixes=0;this.children=[]};Trie.prototype={insert:function(e,t){if(e.length==0){return}var n=this,r,i;if(t===undefined){t=0}if(t===e.length){n.words++;return}n.prefixes++;r=e[t];if(n.children[r]===undefined){n.children[r]=new Trie}i=n.children[r];i.insert(e,t+1)},remove:function(e,t){if(e.length==0){return}var n=this,r,i;if(t===undefined){t=0}if(n===undefined){return}if(t===e.length){n.words--;return}n.prefixes--;r=e[t];i=n.children[r];i.remove(e,t+1)},update:function(e,t){if(e.length==0||t.length==0){return}this.remove(e);this.insert(t)},countWord:function(e,t){if(e.length==0){return 0}var n=this,r,i,s=0;if(t===undefined){t=0}if(t===e.length){return n.words}r=e[t];i=n.children[r];if(i!==undefined){s=i.countWord(e,t+1)}return s},countPrefix:function(e,t){if(e.length==0){return 0}var n=this,r,i,s=0;if(t===undefined){t=0}if(t===e.length){return n.prefixes}var r=e[t];i=n.children[r];if(i!==undefined){s=i.countPrefix(e,t+1)}return s},find:function(e){if(e.length==0){return false}if(this.countWord(e)&gt;0){return true}else{return false}},getAllWords:function(e){var t=this,n,r,i=[];if(e===undefined){e=""}if(t===undefined){return[]}if(t.words&gt;0){i.push(e)}for(n in t.children){r=t.children[n];i=i.concat(r.getAllWords(e+n))}return i},autoComplete:function(e,t){if(e.length==0){return[]}var n=this,r,i;if(t===undefined){t=0}r=e[t];i=n.children[r];if(i===undefined){return[]}if(t===e.length-1){return i.getAllWords(e)}return i.autoComplete(e,t+1)}}

						//http://stackoverflow.com/questions/460070/detecting-mistyped-email-addresses-in-javascript#answer-460102
						levenshteinenator=function(e,t){var n;var r=e.length;var i=t.length;if(r&lt;i){var s=e;e=t;t=s;var o=r;r=i;i=o}var u=new Array;u[0]=new Array;for(var s=0;s&lt;i+1;s++){u[0][s]=s}for(var a=1;a&lt;r+1;a++){u[a]=new Array;u[a][0]=a;for(var f=1;f&lt;i+1;f++){n=e.charAt(a-1)==t.charAt(f-1)?0:1;u[a][f]=minimator(u[a-1][f]+1,u[a][f-1]+1,u[a-1][f-1]+n)}}return u[r][i]};minimator=function(e,t,n){if(e&lt;t&amp;&amp;e&lt;n)return e;if(t&lt;e&amp;&amp;t&lt;n)return t;return n}

						var T = new Trie();

						$.each(LOLKING.champions, function(i, o) {
                            T.insert(o.internal_name.toLowerCase());
                        });

                        var regions = LOLKING.regions;
                        var cookie_name = 'default-region';
                        var initial_region = Cookies.get(cookie_name) || 'none';

                        var $region = $('.tselect-container ul li[data-tselect-value="' + initial_region.toUpperCase() + '"]');

                        var hasPickedRegion = $region.length != 0;

                        if( !hasPickedRegion ) {

                            initial_region = 'na';
                            $('#select-your-region-callout').fadeIn();
                            $region = $('.tselect-container ul li[data-tselect-value="' + initial_region.toUpperCase() + '"]');

                        }

                        var selectedText = $region.attr('data-tselect-selected-label') || $(this).text();
                        var selectedValue = $region.attr('data-tselect-value') || $(this).text();
                        $region.parent().children().first().text(selectedText);
                        $region.parent().parent().find('[type="hidden"]').val(selectedValue);

                        $('.tselect-container ul li:gt(0)').click(function(){

                            Cookies.set(cookie_name, $(this).attr('data-tselect-value').toLowerCase(), {expires: 31536000});
                            $('.suggestive-search-container [name="name"]').trigger('keyup').focus();

                        });

						$('.suggestive-search-container [name="name"]').bind('focus', function(e){
							if( $('#search-suggestions-container').children().length &gt; 0 ) {
								$('#search-suggestions-container').fadeIn();
                                $('.suggestive-search-container').addClass('suggestive-search-container-open');
                                if( !hasPickedRegion ) $('#select-your-region-callout').hide();
							}
						});

						$('.suggestive-search-container [name="name"]').bind('keyup', function(e){

                            if (e.ctrlKey &amp;&amp; e.keyCode == 13) {
                                window.location = $('.search-suggestions-container li:eq(0) a').attr('href');
                                return;
                            }

							if( e.keyCode &amp;&amp; e.keyCode == 27 ) {
								$(this).blur();
								return;
							}

							var str = $("&lt;div/&gt;").text($(this).val()).html();
							var slug = str.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z]/g, "");
							var champion_slug = null;

							var rows = [];

							if( slug.length ) {

								var trie_matches = T.autoComplete(slug);

								if( trie_matches.length ) {

									champion_slug = trie_matches.sort(function (a, b) { return a.length - b.length; })[0];

								} else {

									var closest_champion;
									var closest_champion_score = 10;

									$.each(LOLKING.champions, function(i, o) {
										var score = levenshteinenator(slug, o.internal_name);
										if( score &lt; closest_champion_score ) {
											closest_champion_score = score;
											closest_champion = o.internal_name;
										}

									});

									if( closest_champion_score &lt;= 3 ) {
										champion_slug = closest_champion;
									}

								}

								if( str.length &gt;= 2) {

									var html = [
									'&lt;li&gt;',
										'&lt;a style="position: relative;" href="/now/' + $('.suggestive-search-container [name="region"]').val().toLowerCase()  + '/' + str + '"&gt;',
											'&lt;div style="text-align: left; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);"&gt;Active Game Search&lt;/div&gt;',
											'&lt;p&gt;View current game details for &lt;strong style="color: #FFCD03; font: bold 14px \'Open Sans\';"&gt;' + str +'&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;',
                                            '&lt;span style="font: 11px \'Trebuchet Ms\'; color: #DDD; position: absolute; top: 4px; right: 6px;"&gt;' + (navigator.platform.toUpperCase().indexOf('MAC')&gt;=0 ? 'OPTION+ENTER' : 'CTRL+ENTER') + '&lt;/span&gt;',
										'&lt;/a&gt;',
									'&lt;/li&gt;',
									'&lt;li&gt;',
										'&lt;a href="/search?name=' + str + '"&gt;',
											'&lt;div style="text-align: left; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);"&gt;Search All Regions&lt;/div&gt;',
											'&lt;p&gt;See profiles from all supported regions.&lt;/p&gt;',
										'&lt;/a&gt;',
									'&lt;/li&gt;'
									].join('');

									rows.push(html);

								}


								if( champion_slug &amp;&amp; LOLKING.champions[champion_slug] ) {

									var html = [
									'&lt;li&gt;',
										'&lt;div&gt;',
											'&lt;div style="width: 48px; height: 48px; background: url(//lkimg.zamimg.com/shared/riot/images/champions/' + LOLKING.champions[champion_slug].champion_id + '_64.png) center; border-radius: 6px; box-shadow: 0 0 2px #000; float: left; margin-right: 10px;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;',
											'&lt;div style="float: left;"&gt;',
												'&lt;div style="text-align: left; text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);"&gt;' + LOLKING.champions[champion_slug].name + '&lt;/div&gt;',
												'&lt;p&gt;Check out &lt;a href="/guides/list.php?champion=' + LOLKING.champions[champion_slug].file + '"&gt;guides&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href="/models/?champion=' + LOLKING.champions[champion_slug].champion_id + '&amp;skin=0"&gt;3D models&lt;/a&gt;, and &lt;a href="/champions/' + LOLKING.champions[champion_slug].file + '#statistics"&gt;statistics&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;',
											'&lt;/div&gt;',
										'&lt;/div&gt;',
									'&lt;/li&gt;'
									].join('');

									rows.push(html);

								}
							}

							$('.search-suggestions-container').empty().html(rows.join(''));

							if( $('.search-suggestions-container').children().length &gt; 0 ) {
								$('.search-suggestions-container').fadeIn();
                                $('.suggestive-search-container').addClass('suggestive-search-container-open');
                                if( !hasPickedRegion ) $('#select-your-region-callout').hide();
							} else {
								$('.search-suggestions-container').hide();
                                $('.suggestive-search-container').removeClass('suggestive-search-container-open');
                                if( !hasPickedRegion ) $('#select-your-region-callout').fadeIn();
							}

						});

					});

								   	$('.toggle-btn').click(function(){

								      var start = 0;
								      var end = 35;
								      var animate_from = [95, 171, 57];
								      var animate_to = [50, 50, 50]; // paint it black    

								      var $block = $(this);
								      if( $block.is(':animated') ) return;

								      if( $block.attr('data-toggle') == "off" ) {
								         start = 35;
								         end = -35;
								         animate_to = [95, 171, 57];
								         animate_from = [50, 50, 50];
								         $block.attr('data-toggle', "on");

								        $('#table-mode').hide();
								        $('#interactive-mode').show();

								        Cookies.set(cookie_name, 'interactive', {expires: 31536000});

								       } else {
								         $block.attr('data-toggle', "off");

								        $('#table-mode').show();
								        $('#interactive-mode').hide();

								             ];
								 
								             $block.css('backgroundColor', 'rgb(' + rgb.join(',') + ')');
								 
								           },
								           easing: 'easeInOutCirc',
								           duration: 200
								         });
								 
								     });

                                    $('.rune-model').click(function(e){
                                      e.preventDefault();
                                      var idx = $(this).attr('data-idx');
                                      if( rune_pages[idx] ) {
                                        $.tmodal({
                                            content: Mustache.to_html($('#rune-page-template').html(), rune_pages[idx]), 
                                            showCloseBtn: true, 
                                            closeOnMaskClick: true,
                                            closeOnEsc: true,
                                            onOpen: function(){
                                                LOLKING.tooltips.update();
                                            }
                                        });
                                      }
                                    }).each(function(){
                                    
                                        var idx = $(this).attr('data-idx');
                                    
                                        var tt = $.map(rune_pages[idx].statistics, function(o) {
                                            return "&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td style=\"text-align: right; padding-right: 4px;\"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;" + o.label + "&lt;/strong&gt;:&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=\"text-align: left;\"&gt;" + o.description + "&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;";
                                        }).join("");
                                        
                                        tt = "&lt;table style=\"margin: 0; padding: 0;\"&gt;" + tt + "&lt;/table&gt;";
                                        
                                        tt = "&lt;div style=\"font-size: 12px;\"&gt;" + tt + "&lt;/div&gt;";
                                        
                                        tt += "&lt;div style=\"margin-top: 10px; text-transform: uppercase; color: #999;\"&gt;Click for full details&lt;/div&gt;";
                                    
                                        $(this).tipsy({
                                            html: true,
                                            gravity: 's',
                                            offset: 4,
                                            fallback: tt
                                        });
                                    
                                    });

                                    $('.mastery-model').click(function(e){
                                      e.preventDefault();
                                      var idx = $(this).attr('data-idx');
                                      if( mastery_pages[idx] ) {
                                        $.tmodal({
                                            content: Mustache.to_html($('#mastery-page-s4-template').html(), mastery_pages[idx]), 
                                            showCloseBtn: true, 
                                            closeOnMaskClick: true,
                                            closeOnEsc: true,
                                            onOpen: function(){
                                                LOLKING.tooltips.update();
                                            }
                                        });
                                      }
                                    }).each(function(){
                                    
                                        var idx = $(this).attr('data-idx');
                                    
                                        var tt = "&lt;div style=\"text-transform: uppercase; color: #999;\"&gt;Click for full details&lt;/div&gt;";
                                        
                                        $(this).tipsy({
                                            html: true,
                                            gravity: 's',
                                            offset: 4,
                                            fallback: tt
                                        });
                                    
                                    });       

                                    $('.queued_alone').parent().attr('title', 'Queued Alone').tipsy({
                                        gravity: 's',
                                        offset: 4
                                    });
                            
                            
                                    $('#table-mode .queued_together').each(function(){

                                    	$(this).closest('td').hover(function(){

	                                    	var teamId = $(this).find('.queued_together').attr('data-queue_team_id');
	                                    	$('#table-mode .queued_together[data-queue_team_id="' + teamId + '"]').closest('tr').addClass('highlight');

	                                    }, function() {

	                                    	var teamId = $(this).find('.queued_together').attr('data-queue_team_id');
	                                    	$('#table-mode .queued_together[data-queue_team_id="' + teamId + '"]').closest('tr').removeClass('highlight');

	                                    });

                                    });

                                    $('#table-mode, #interactive-mode').each(function(){
                            
                                        if( $(this).find('.queued_together').length ) {
                                        
                                            var current_team_num = 1;
                                            var team_num_map = {};
                                            var $p = $(this);
                                            $(this).find('.queued_together').each(function(){
                                            
                                                var queue_team_id = $(this).attr('data-queue_team_id');
                                                var queue_team_num;
                                                
                                                if( team_num_map[queue_team_id] ) {
                                                    queue_team_num = team_num_map[queue_team_id];
                                                } else {
                                                    queue_team_num = current_team_num++;
                                                    team_num_map[queue_team_id] = queue_team_num;
                                                }



                                                $(this).parent().attr('title', "Queued with: " + $.map($p.find('.queued_together[data-queue_team_id="' + queue_team_id + '"]').not(this), function(el, i) {
                                                    return $(el).attr('data-name');
                                                }).join(', ')).tipsy({
                                                    gravity: 's',
                                                    offset: 4
                                                }).addClass('queued_together'+queue_team_num);
                                            
                                            });
                                        
                                        }
                                    
                                    });                                    
                                    
                                });

                            </script>

<script>

$(function(){
    $('.toggle-btn').click(function(){

      var start = 0;
      var end = 35;
      var animate_from = [95, 171, 57];
      var animate_to = [50, 50, 50]; // paint it black    

      var $block = $(this);
      if( $block.is(':animated') ) return;

      if( $block.attr('data-toggle') == "off" ) {
         start = 35;
         end = -35;
         animate_to = [95, 171, 57];
         animate_from = [50, 50, 50];
         $block.attr('data-toggle', "on");

        $('#table-mode').hide();
        $('#interactive-mode').show();

        //Cookies.set(cookie_name, 'interactive', {expires: 31536000});

       } else {
         $block.attr('data-toggle', "off");

        $('#table-mode').show();
        $('#interactive-mode').hide();

        //Cookies.set(cookie_name, 'table', {expires: 31536000});

       }
     
       var $toggle = $(this).find('.toggle-btn-switch');
 
       $block.css({ orphans: 0 })
         .animate({ orphans: 1 }, {
           step: function(n, fx) {
 
             $toggle.css('left', (start+(end*n)) + 'px');
 
             var rgb = [
               Math.floor(animate_from[0] + ((animate_to[0] - animate_from[0]) * n)),
               Math.floor(animate_from[1] + ((animate_to[1] - animate_from[1]) * n)),
               Math.floor(animate_from[2] + ((animate_to[2] - animate_from[2]) * n))
             ];
 
             $block.css('backgroundColor', 'rgb(' + rgb.join(',') + ')');
 
           },
           easing: 'easeInOutCirc',
           duration: 200
         });
 
     });

});

</script>
